      rm -f libgphoto2_port-10.1po libgphoto2_port-10.2po libgphoto2_port-10.po; \

  if test -f ../../po/libgphoto2-6.pot; then \
    sed -f remove-potcdate.sed < ../../po/libgphoto2-6.pot > libgphoto2-6.1po && \
    sed -f remove-potcdate.sed < libgphoto2-6.po > libgphoto2-6.2po && \
    if cmp libgphoto2-6.1po libgphoto2-6.2po >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
      rm -f libgphoto2-6.1po libgphoto2-6.2po libgphoto2-6.po; \
    else \
      rm -f libgphoto2-6.1po libgphoto2-6.2po ../../po/libgphoto2-6.pot && \
      mv libgphoto2-6.po ../../po/libgphoto2-6.pot; \
    fi; \
  else \
    mv libgphoto2-6.po ../../po/libgphoto2-6.pot; \
  fi; \
}
